  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a6322bdb-466e-4847-a33f-ae731affe3e7'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText6348728641823495436" style="display:none"><b>Is love in the cards?</b><br /><br />Since birth, Lexie Berry has had nothing but bad luck. Orphaned at an early age, she had a rough childhood and a boyfriend who was murdered. Now the beautiful, stylish Lexie is determined to change her luck and her life. But first she's got to make good on a promise: to pick up Ty Walker from prison. One look at the gorgeous ex-convict and Lexie knows she's in trouble-and already thinking about taking a walk on the wild side . . . <br /><br />For five years, Ty was imprisoned for a crime he didn't commit. Now he wants revenge on the people who framed him. Yet when the high-stakes poker player sees the leggy Lexie, he suddenly has other desires on his mind. Realizing that Ty is innocent, Lexie tries to stop his plan for vengeance and help him become a better man. But as Ty battles his inner demons, dirty cops and criminals plot to take him out. Can he and Lexie find a way to escape the past?</span>

        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('edition_18773958').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('edition_18773958').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('edition_18773958').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {

<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/585910-why-is-this-book-so-racist-am-i-the-only">Why is this book so racist? Am I the only one who was uncomfortable reading this?</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_585910'><a id="like_count_community_question_585910" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/585910?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">9 likes</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F12958487-lady-luck">like</a></span>

</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionTimestamp'>
<a href="/questions/585910-why-is-this-book-so-racist-am-i-the-only">5 years ago</a>
</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionPermalink'>
<a href="/questions/585910-why-is-this-book-so-racist-am-i-the-only">See all 7 answers</a>
</li>
</ul>
</div>

</div>
<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/18146613-izu"><img alt="" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_100x100-6433b08cbe793211f55e184d39e84c4d.png" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/18146613-izu">Izu</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Well, yes and no. I'm referring to the constant almost macabre stereotyping. The fact that the only full-black male has three women he's sleeping with<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Well, yes and no. I'm referring to the constant almost macabre stereotyping. The fact that the only full-black male has three women he's sleeping with. The fact that Ty likes gansta rap. The fact that everything that he is is defined by the color of his skin, and not much else. I understand that KA's heroes are usually assholes; it's her thing. You get it or you don't. But why is it that the dishes the women made were so...black. Like what the actual fuck, black people only eat cornbread and grits, right? And why the fuck is Lex so special because she fucks black guys? Is she taking one for the white girl team? Is there something better about lowering oneself to permit a black cock to enter her? I'm sorry but what the fuck. Lines were crossed, and nobody seems to have a problem with the constant stuffing of black people into KA's stereotype box. That's what I mean by why is this book so racist.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2887549165035768581"><b>5 LUCKY Stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/a1640d49-0840-4d13-b144-b70bbb92344b_zps0e0a3dc0.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382276054i/5784192.jpg' alt=' photo a1640d49-0840-4d13-b144-b70bbb92344b_zps0e0a3dc0.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Just when I thought it couldn't get any better than Tate's book in the Colorado Mountain series... well, I was wrong! Ty and Lexie's book was just as good, maybe even better! I absolutely LOVED it!<br/><br/> Ty and Lexie did things backwards... within 48 hours of meeting each other, they were married. Ty just got out of a 5 year stent in prison for a crime he did not commit. Lexie is doing a favor for a low life who was friends with her dead boyfriend. They married for appearances only, </span>
  <span id="freeText2887549165035768581" style="display:none"><b>5 LUCKY Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/a1640d49-0840-4d13-b144-b70bbb92344b_zps0e0a3dc0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382276054i/5784192.jpg" alt=" photo a1640d49-0840-4d13-b144-b70bbb92344b_zps0e0a3dc0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Just when I thought it couldn't get any better than Tate's book in the Colorado Mountain series... well, I was wrong! Ty and Lexie's book was just as good, maybe even better! I absolutely LOVED it!<br><br> Ty and Lexie did things backwards... within 48 hours of meeting each other, they were married. Ty just got out of a 5 year stent in prison for a crime he did not commit. Lexie is doing a favor for a low life who was friends with her dead boyfriend. They married for appearances only, or at least thats how it starts... <br><br>Lexie and Ty together... I loved it! Lexie is one of the best KA heroines. Sweet, fun, hilarious, giving, nurturing, and yes, goofy. Not annoying at in the least! Ty loved her goofiness...<br><i>
  <blockquote>"You're part-goof all class. Never walked in a room, any room, with a woman on my arm, any woman, who's got your looks, your style, the kinda beauty you got and the light that shines from you. So I don't get it. I don't get how a woman leads a life full of shit and comes out of it bein' part-goof and all class. That shit's impossible but there you fuckin' are. Part-goof, all class." <br>I felt my breath coming fast but managed to whisper, "I'm not part-goof." <br>"You're right. I was bein' nice. You're a total goof." <br>"Am not" </blockquote>
</i><br>Ty is another hot alpha man... Mmm just the description of him, I loved him right off the bat! He could be a jerk at times, but he had it rough. I think anyone would have that attitude if they were locked up for that long for something they didn’t do. The more you get to know the real Ty, the more you will love him. He is really a thoughtful and sweet man. <br><i>
  <blockquote>My Ty. <br>My Ty. <br>Christ. Fuck. <br>Christ. <br>Two words. Just two words. Walker had no clue until that moment that two words could mean so fucking much. He'd never belonged to anyone. He'd never belonged anywhere. Never thought he wanted to. <br>Until he heard those two words. </blockquote>
</i> The mama nickname... I just adored it!<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/0817b712-f7a0-4403-829f-1d19f013f2f3_zps15a3e0e1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382552859i/5983274.jpg" alt=" photo 0817b712-f7a0-4403-829f-1d19f013f2f3_zps15a3e0e1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Even though Ty and Lexie got together in a totally unconventional way, I loved how they really meshed well, worked together and became a team.<br><i>
  <blockquote>‘This is is, Team Walker, you and me. We want somethin’, we find a way to get it. We hit a rough patch, we find a way to get over it. We face a challenge, we find a way to beat it. It’s good, we savor it. What I’m sayin’ is, this team is a winner. We never forget to celebrate the victories and we get a lotta those because we never admit defeat.’</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/71cfa0cf-2661-4048-9358-0fdbdad28999_zps5e831e1a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382552859i/5983275.jpg" alt=" photo 71cfa0cf-2661-4048-9358-0fdbdad28999_zps5e831e1a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I can’t think of much I didn’t love in this story... there was the perfect amount of humor, romance, drama, conflict and sexiness. Overall, it was a fantastic read! Can’t wait to get to Breathe!<br><br>My favorite line &lt;3 <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Your nightmare, mama, was my dream." <br>My heart clenched. <br>He kept going. "Never had a home until you gave me one." <br>My breath started sticking. <br>"Never had anyone give to me the way you gave to me." <br>My breath stopped sticking and clogged. <br>"Never thought of findin' a woman who I wanted to have my baby." <br>Oh God. <br>"Never had light in my life, never, not once, I lived wild but I didn't burn bright until you shined your light on me." </blockquote>
  </b>
</i> This is a MUST READ for me!!! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/dfbddaa9-752b-490f-9a31-02c7cb814040_zpsaec53cc7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382552859i/5983276.jpg" alt=" photo dfbddaa9-752b-490f-9a31-02c7cb814040_zpsaec53cc7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1618009537" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2507102684461555017"><b> 4.5 Team Walker Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/10405397_zpsuwbkfzsg.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462801034ra/19045450.gif' alt=' photo 10405397_zpsuwbkfzsg.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>Some Spoilers</b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>“You’re part-goof all class. Never walked in a room, any room, with a woman on my arm, any woman, who’s got your looks, your style, the kinda beauty you got and the light that shines from you. So I don’t get it. I don’t get how a woman leads a life full of shit and comes out of it bein’ part-goof and all class. That shit’s impossible but there you fuckin’ are. Part-goof, all class.”-Ty</b>
</i><br/><br/>Lady Luck was so good. I think it is tied with Max's book for my favo</span>
  <span id="freeText2507102684461555017" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 Team Walker Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/10405397_zpsuwbkfzsg.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462801034ra/19045450.gif" alt=" photo 10405397_zpsuwbkfzsg.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Some Spoilers</b><br><br><i>
  <b>“You’re part-goof all class. Never walked in a room, any room, with a woman on my arm, any woman, who’s got your looks, your style, the kinda beauty you got and the light that shines from you. So I don’t get it. I don’t get how a woman leads a life full of shit and comes out of it bein’ part-goof and all class. That shit’s impossible but there you fuckin’ are. Part-goof, all class.”-Ty</b>
</i><br><br>Lady Luck was so good. I think it is tied with Max's book for my favorite of the series so far. It was intense and exciting. There was more then just the Ty and Lexie love story. There was a very exciting dirty cops side story that also really held my interest. Ty and Lexie's love story was so good I kept finding myself reading ahead to get a peek at what was to come. <br><br><i>
  <b>“Don’t!” she snapped. “Don’t you fucking come home and think you can give me a different Ty. Do not think you can fucking play me like that. I don’t know what the fuck you’re dealing with and I don’t care. I asked, you wouldn’t tell me. I tried everything I knew to get you to let me in there,” she jabbed her finger at his chest, “and you didn’t let me in and now, Ty, I don’t fucking care. You can ride the wave of whatever’s controlling you but don’t drag me along on that trip.” She swung her arm out to the side. “Out there, I’ll be what you’re paying me to be.” Then she pointed to the floor. “In here, it would be good if we could be civil to each other and you don’t give me any of that pussy bullshit of yours. And that’s all for in here, Ty. Tonight, I sleep on the couch and I keep doing it until my bed gets here and then I’ll move to it. You wanted to talk, there it is. I’m laying it out. You don’t like that, you get your bling back and I walk. Think about it and enjoy the spaghetti, I’m going for a drive.”-Lex</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/BeFunky%20Collagejashd_zpslmdrhdak.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462801034i/19045451._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo BeFunky Collagejashd_zpslmdrhdak.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b>“Let me go.” He moved his lips to her ear and whispered, “I hurt you, baby.” Her body went still in his arms and she whispered back, “Don’t.” “I was a dick; I fucked up and hurt you.” “Stop it.” He tightened his arms and pressed his temple into her hair. It was soft as well as thick and smelled fucking great. He wanted his hands in it. He wanted to feel it on his skin. He wanted to feel it all around as her mouth worked his cock. “I’m sorry I hurt you, Lexie,” he murmured into her hair. “Please stop it.”-Lex and Ty</b>
</i><br><br>Ty was a hard man. He was just getting out of prison after losing 5 years of his life for a crime he didn't commit. Dirty cops in his town set him up with the help of his ex to take the fall for another dirty cop. All because he was half black and they didn't like color. To say he was bitter and mad as hell was a understatement. He formed a plan to get married to a woman that is clean to be his alibi so he can get his revenge and she'd have his back covered. So right before he was released he called in a favor from a POS drug dealer and pimp that owes him one. That favor, send him a woman that isn't a druggie or whore that he can marry for an alibi. So when he stepped out of the prison he was greeted by Lexie. Lexie was beautiful, goofy, and her soul shined bright. He wanted her but soon learned that she thought she was just suppose to pick him up from prison and drop him off. So he made her an offer. Become his wife for 50k, just while he handles his business. But soon after he married her, he decided he wanted to keep her. Ty was protective, could be sweet but he could be a dick too. But when Ty was wrong he would man up and say sorry. He also gave it his all when he decided he wanted the real thing with Lexie. He did his best to make her happy and keep her safe from his past. Ty was a yummy sexy crude mouth beast and I fell in love with him. <br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/tumblr_mjykzuwHfK1qfj6oyo1_r1_500_zpse20vxtuw.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462801034ra/19045452.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mjykzuwHfK1qfj6oyo1_r1_500_zpse20vxtuw.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b>“How is this getting me dirty?” “Lexie, it comes down to it, I’ll be askin’ you to lie to cops.” “Ty, it comes down to it, I’ll be lying to dirty cops and everyone knows a double negative is a positive.”-Lex and Ty</b>
</i><br><br><br>Lexie has had a rough life. No family and from foster care, her one and only love her boyfriend Ronnie was killed, shot 7 times for living the wrong kind of life. She was mad at him and herself for not walking away. Now because of the circles her ex ran in she was under the thumb of a drug dealing pimp name Shift. So when she was asked to pick up a guy getting out of prison and take him where he wants to go she felt like she had no choice but to do it. After she picked up the yumminess that was Ty she realized she got played by Shift and that he gave her to Ty to be his wife because Shift owed him. Ty instead offers her a deal. Become his wife and he will pay her 50k and get her out from under Shift's thumb forever. So she took the deal knowing it would give her the new start she has been working for. 2 days in and she fell in love with her husband, who could be hard, closed off but giving and thoughtful. Lexie decided she was going to give him a home since he had 5 years of his life stolen from him. She was supportive, sweet and goofy. She wanted to make him smile and laugh. As much as I loved Ty and I did I loved Lexie more. She had that something special about her that really shined through the pages and felt tangible.<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/tumblr_inline_ndejyxvWpB1rdych8_zpsqswvjfc8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462801034ra/19045453.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_ndejyxvWpB1rdych8_zpsqswvjfc8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><i>
  <b>“Drama over, we’re back to us and I didn’t just fuck up, I did it huge, I said nasty shit that shouldn’t have been said and I can’t take that back. The wounds I inflicted went deep and I can only hope to Christ one day they heal over. Until that day, mama, all I can promise you is that I’ll do all I can do to beat that shit back and never do that to you again. But we got a rocky road ahead of us and I don’t know where it’s gonna lead before we get to the other side. The only thing I can give you is, that shit comes outta my mouth and cuts you, you gotta understand that shit was planted in me and I gotta get it out. I’ll try to do it in a way that doesn’t harm you but I obviously am not battin’ a thousand with that so I can make no promises except I’ll try. What you need to give me is to know it is not about you, it’s about me, you gotta suck it up and stand by me, you gotta know, in the end, I’ll work my ass off to make it all worth it to you and you gotta always remember I love you and I have never, not once, said those words to any breathing soul so you also gotta know what that means.”-Ty</b>
</i><br><br><br>Lexie and Ty's relationship was raw, intense and passionate. They had each others backs. Were supportive and gave their all to the relationship. There was some sweet and funny moments in their relationship, some really sexy moments and there were some moments that ripped my heart out. One of the things I loved about this book is there is a lot of Tate in this book. We get to see Krystal, bubba, Jim billy, Laurie, Jonas, Deke and Wood again too. I loved that Wood is back with his ex but I'm confused because I looked ahead in this series and I seen that wood gets his own book. How does he get a book if he and Mag are together? One thing I think really makes this series awesome is the amazing secondary characters KA writes. I mean the heroes are yummy and super alpha the heroine are sassy, and trendy, but the secondary characters have so much depth and heart I can't help but fall love with them all. This book was a total winner for me. I loved Lex, Ty and every minute of their story. Their Hea was perfect. I can't wait to start the next book!<br><br><i>
  <b>“This is it, Team Walker, you and me. We want somethin’, we find a way to get it. We hit a rough patch, we find a way to get over it. We face a challenge, we find a way to beat it. It’s good, we savor it. What I’m sayin’ is, this team is a winner. We never forget to celebrate the victories and we get a lotta those because we never admit defeat.”-Ty</b>
</i><br></span>

    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/276470580?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=2012-reads">2012-reads</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=format-ebook-borrowed">format-ebook-borrowed</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer276470580" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3844829763934393998"><br/><i>Lady Luck </i> is the third book in the <i>Colorado Mountain</i> series and, in my opinion, has the best storyline of the three. I adore Ty Walker who, if you can believe it, is even more crass and foul mouthed than either Max or Tate… or maybe even both Max and Tate combined! So yeah, be prepared, because this book takes crassiness to a whole new level! In fact, I made up a word to describe Ty – crasshat… a crass asshat… And I wouldn't change a thing about him.<br/><br/>So, let’s break it down. What is it that has </span>
  <span id="freeText3844829763934393998" style="display:none"><br /><i>Lady Luck </i> is the third book in the <i>Colorado Mountain</i> series and, in my opinion, has the best storyline of the three. I adore Ty Walker who, if you can believe it, is even more crass and foul mouthed than either Max or Tate… or maybe even both Max and Tate combined! So yeah, be prepared, because this book takes crassiness to a whole new level! In fact, I made up a word to describe Ty – crasshat… a crass asshat… And I wouldn't change a thing about him.<br /><br />So, let’s break it down. What is it that has me loving this book? <br /><br />1.	Ty might be a crasshat, but he’s not a stupid crasshat. He uses the smarts God gave him and doesn’t put the people he loves in danger (much) even though it means putting his plans for a much deserved revenge on hold.<br /><br />2.	Lexie Berry is a great heroine. Smart, independent, and never TSTL (Too Stupid To Live). She’s a woman who is 100% devoted to her loved ones, even if they don’t always deserve it.<br /><br />3.	The. Sex. Is. Hot. I mean, Burn. Up. The. Pages. Hot. (In my opinion.)<br /><br />4.	Fantastic story. Heartwarming, exciting, believable… loved it.<br /><br />5.	We see a lot of Tate and Wood. (Woot!)<br /><br />6. Had me in tears.<br /><br />7. One of the best, most heartbreaking scenes ever written! Not too spoiler: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br /><br /><i>“Just go,”</i> I hissed. “Fuck, Ty, if I make the decision that I want to just be, can’t I just fucking <i>be </i>without all this fucking <i>bullshit</i>? My grandfather controlled my life and with that, I had no choice. Then Ronnie did and with that, I did but did I make the right choice? No. Then Shift controlled it and my choices were limited but I still didn’t make the right ones. Can you give me one fucking thing in this nightmare and let me make my own fucking choice?”<br /><br />When I was done speaking I felt his body had gone still again, stone still.<br /><br />And silent.<br /><br />Then he asked quietly, “Nightmare?”<br /><br />“Nightmare,” I replied firmly.<br /><br />Ty didn’t move.<br /><br />By a miracle, I held it together.<br /><br />Then he moved but it was to rest his chin on my shoulder and I closed my eyes because I needed him to go, go, <i>go</i> so I could fall apart again on my own.<br /><br />Then he said, “Your nightmare, mama, was my dream.”<br /><br />My heart clenched.<br /><br />He kept going. “Never had a home until you gave me one.”<br /><br />My breath started sticking.<br /><br />“Never had anyone give to me the way you gave to me.”<br /><br />My breath stopped sticking and clogged.<br /><br />“Never thought of findin’ a woman who I wanted to have my baby.”<br /><br />Oh <i>God.</i><br /><br />“Never had light in my life, never, not once, I lived wild but I didn’t burn bright until you shined your light on me.”<br /><br /><i>Oh God.</i><br /><br />“Whacked, fuckin’ insane, but, at night, you curled in front of me, didn’t mind I did that time that wasn’t mine ‘cause it meant I walked out to you.”<br /><br />He had to stop. He <i>had</i> to.<br /><br />He didn’t.<br /><br />“Your nightmare,” he whispered, turned his head and against my neck he finished, “my dream.”<br /><br />Then he kissed my neck, gave me one last squeeze of his long, strong, powerful arms then he let me go, shifted back, got to his feet and I heard his footsteps walking away. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I cried the first time I read that and I cry still when I think of it.<br /><br />*sigh*<br /><br />But yeah, another great, great story!<br /><br />-----<br />If you're a Kristen Ashley addict, or just interested in checking her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads! <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3844829763934393998" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_416700508" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/416700508" />
    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/416700508?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/22920665-lady-luck">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=kristen-ashley">kristen-ashley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=best-of-the-bestest">best-of-the-bestest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=cont-series">cont-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=audio">audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer416700508" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2341050471545894485">October 16, 2018<br/><br/>Here we are again and it's amazing that a book I've re-read/listen over and over still gives me the same KA high that I love. Honestly, there is NO other author I re-read as much or as often as Kristen Ashley. Lady Luck is one of my favourites and I'm sure I will be back again next year.<br/><br/>*********<br/>July 17, 2017. Re-read/listen to for the 20 billionth time and I still love it. How is it that a Kristen Ashley re-read still gives me happy buzz's and the shakes and shiveries?<br/><br/>**********</span>
  <span id="freeText2341050471545894485" style="display:none">October 16, 2018<br><br>Here we are again and it's amazing that a book I've re-read/listen over and over still gives me the same KA high that I love. Honestly, there is NO other author I re-read as much or as often as Kristen Ashley. Lady Luck is one of my favourites and I'm sure I will be back again next year.<br><br>*********<br>July 17, 2017. Re-read/listen to for the 20 billionth time and I still love it. How is it that a Kristen Ashley re-read still gives me happy buzz's and the shakes and shiveries?<br><br>**********<br><br><b>Something to talk about...</b><br><br><i>***This review will be REALLY spoilerish. I decided to put my thoughts down without holding back worrying about spoilers. I loved this book and if you agreed or disagreed with any of my thoughts, I'd love to discuss them in the comments. So shut this sucker down if you haven't read Lady Luck and you plan to, but make sure to come back for a chat when you've finished it. ***</i><br><br>First off...I love that Epilogue. Seriously, it was one of KA's best by far. Talk of babies, what's going on with everyone, who survived, who didn't, who has found love and who is happy to just be an observer to the happiness and love surrounding them. Sitting down to a Thanksgiving with all the characters you've loved or learned to love. Seeing Lexie at her goofiest, Ty at his sweetest and their friends happy and content to be around loved ones. I FREAKIN LOVED IT!! (channelling a little KA there).<br><br>Now, I was a little hesitant to start the audio of Lady Luck because I didn't want my happy memories to be dashed by a shoddy narrator. Luckily, I ended up having no problems with it at all. The narrator did a great job as she spoke very clearly, and I was able to tell when characters changed easily. I think, in my case, the accents weren't an issue because they are not ones I hear a lot so have no basis to compare. I don't come across big, American, mountain men on the streets of Brisbane Australia. So if Ty's accent is wrong or if Pena's was wrong, I can't judge. So overall, I enjoyed the audio of <i>Lady Luck</i>.<br><br>Now...time to talk Lady Luck. This book is packed full of emotions that can take you from the highest high to the lowest low. We are faced with characters who have not had the easiest life, but still manage to keep on keeping on. They recognise and have lived with injustice. Neither Lexie or Ty had good parents as role models. Luckily for both of them,they found good people who were willing to give them guidance and support they lacked at home. What makes Ty and Lexie exceptional characters is their strength and perseverance considering their negative and bad upbringings. Straight up...I loved these characters. <br><br>The beginning of the story where Ty and Lexie meet and get to know each other gave me such a goofy grin on my face. This is one of the best stories for a re-read/listen. You get excited when the good parts come (THE SHOWER SCENE) and you get sentimental when a part you know will have more meaning later in the book (the little notes) comes up. My chest puffs up with pride for Lexie when she pulls out her earrings (not knowing she just increased the believability of Ty's scam, but doing it because she's a sweetheart) in the scene at the tables and I love seeing the little glimpse of Ty's potential when he gets the vase for Lexie's flowers. These little things are what makes this book come alive for me. Even if I read this book or listened to this story 100 times, I think I'd still get that same buzz.<br><br><i>Lady Luck</i> still has one of my most favourite scenes of any book I've ever read...the beach scene. Ty knows he has made a monumental mistake and needs Lexie to know how he feels. Now while that scene was one of my favourites, the scene that caused that one to happen, when Ty lashes out (with words) at Lexie, still manages to break my heart every time I read/listen to it. Later on, I wanted to kill Julius for causing Lexie heartbreak, but I loved Ty's reaction to it all. His arms wrapping around Lexie not just to comfort her, but to protect her from Julius's betrayal. Yes, Julius has success in getting them back together, but at first, I couldn't stand the pain Lexie had to deal with and what she had to recover from. I did get there in the end because I know Julius thought he was doing the right thing. He's a bloke, so, of course, he didn't understand or maybe didn't gauge the emotional devastation his actions would bring.<br><br>What Misty Keaton did is one of the evilest and self-serving things I've ever read. I absolutely HATED her...but then I felt sorry for her. Then, I felt guilty for feeling sorry for her. Then, I didn't feel guilty for feeling sorry for her because I remembered what I'd read in Breathe on how she was murdered. Guilty or not, no-one deserves to die that way. Chace Keaton is a character I struggle with. Even after reading <i>Breathe</i> I still struggled with him a little. He made some really dodgy decisions and completely disregarded his marriage vows. I mean, I understand why...but in some ways, I don't. I think I'll have to re-read or maybe listen to <i>Breathe</i> to see if that will help.<br><br><i>Lady Luck</i> deals with a lot of betrayal. Parents who don't do their job right. The law not being upheld because of crooked cops. Friendships and family members who took advantage of their loved ones. While we had plenty of examples of what greed and selfishness can do, we also had shining examples of what good people can and will do. Samuel Sterling with his romantic heart. Detective Pena with his need to make sure that justice is equal whether you are a black or white. Tate who always has his man's back. Ella, Bessy and Honey...not of blood but definitely family to Lexie. I enjoy seeing people come together to do good and when Ty's mates have a welcome home party when he got out of jail, and then when they are all there with the house check/inspection by Fuller, it just reinforces that there are good people out there.<br><br>Wow...the sex scenes...oh my lordy!! Sitting in my car and listening to Ty and Lexie getting it on...I had shivers up my spine. Look, I'm not a huge fan of the "mama", but in Ty's case his actions were WAY better than words.<br><br>I'm sure there are plenty of other things I could talk about from <i>Lady Luck</i> but I'd be here all day (and probably tomorrow) coming up with more reasons why I love it. I love that Lexie has had it tough but manages to find her happy place in a man who walked out of a prison with revenge on his mind. I adored that such a big, tough man who had 5 years taken from him, walked out to a woman who would blur the memories of those 5 years and make a life where his biggest worry was painting over nail polish on the walls, or standing on glitter pens.<br><br>I'll be taking a break from listening to the <i>Colorado Men Series</i> because <i>WILDEST DREAMS</i> (Fantasyland #1) comes out next week. Once I've finished that, I think I'll be listening to the audio of Breathe.<br><br><br><b>I’m an Aussie chick who loves to read and review romance, drink coffee, be a <i>Style Setter</i> and stalk David Gandy. To see more of my reviews, fashion, food and pervathons -</b><br><br><a href="http://staceyissassy.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447925695i/17069306.jpg" width="170" height="170" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/Sassyreviews" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004243.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.pinterest.com/Stacey1565/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004244.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.twitter.com/StaceyisSassy" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004245.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12340912605580212702"><b> 4 Stars <i>(Originally read 4/24/2014) </i></b><br/><br/><b> 4 Stars <i>(Re-read 1/23/2017)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 4 Stars <i>(*Another Re-read 12/6/18*)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 4 Stars <i>(**Another Re-read 7/8/2019**)</i></b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This was an enjoyable re-read. I found that I didn't remember every single detail, so it was nice to read again. I liked experiencing their progression into love. I also liked how Ty melted from being a cold, closed off man into one that loved Lexie openly and was affectionate with her. Because of the revenge aspect this did have a lot of o</span>
  <span id="freeText12340912605580212702" style="display:none"><b> 4 Stars <i>(Originally read 4/24/2014) </i></b><br /><br /><b> 4 Stars <i>(Re-read 1/23/2017)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 4 Stars <i>(*Another Re-read 12/6/18*)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 4 Stars <i>(**Another Re-read 7/8/2019**)</i></b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This was an enjoyable re-read. I found that I didn't remember every single detail, so it was nice to read again. I liked experiencing their progression into love. I also liked how Ty melted from being a cold, closed off man into one that loved Lexie openly and was affectionate with her. Because of the revenge aspect this did have a lot of other stuff going on, but I appreciated how KA still took the time to develop the relationship and focus on the romance in between it all. <br /><br />*I don't have much to add here, but I did get rather bored at the 80ish% point and started to skim. I might have been just anxiously waiting for the cute epilogue...so I'm not going to change my rating at this point*<br /><br />**Again, I don't have much to add. I started this as an audiobook on a roadtrip and ended with reading my ebook copy. I did feel the same need to start skimming around 80ish% as I did on the last re-read, but I think this remains one of my all time favorite epilogues!**<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Lexie and Ty's story. They meet when Lexie picks up Ty from prison. She is stuck under the thumb of an unsavory man after her long-time boyfriend died, and she is made to do jobs for him like picking up Ty. Ty has been released after serving 5 years for a crime he didn't commit, and he has vengeance to get against the men that put him there. He didn't expect Lexie to be the one to pick him up. After propositioning Lexie, he gets her to agree to marrying him in exchange for an escape from the man that has control over her life. Soon they find that the lines between a fake marriage and a real relationship are blurred and they fall in love. There are some big obstacles they have to get through to find their happiness...but they do get a HEA in the end.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between Lexie and Ty's POV (with a few sections in other side character's POV).<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. I never skimmed, and I thought it flowed well. As with most KA books, it is on the longer side - listed as 664 pages on Amazon.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> Yes, but not in the way that I found it unbelievable (and not expressed until close to the end that they were feeling love since the beginning).<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Ty. I loved him until he messed up and pushed the h away. I did think he made up for his mistakes in the end, but I hated the way he reacted.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4 stars. Lexie. She was a good combination of sweet, loyal, sassy, and loving. I only wished that she made Ty work a little harder for her forgiveness.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b> Moderate. I cried in this one. It never turned into ugly crying, and I never needed tissues though.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The H was majorly burned in the past by the last woman he was with (even if she was only a f-buddy), so he pushes the h away a couple times due to his trauma with that. They both pursue the relationship at times. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Moderate. They ave some hot chemistry and scenes, but not so much it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> Not really <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They don't use condoms. There is mention of birth control, but only when the H wants the h to go off of it. No mention of previous practices. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Not in the usual sense. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The H was framed and his ex f-buddy was involved, and she has an uncomfortable interaction with the h. Also, the h's ex died and left her in a bad place with his illegal dealings. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b>No<br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated for ~6 weeks. There is no mention or suggestion of other partners during this time.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ False imprisonment, murder, prostitution, drugs, corruption, blackmail, domestic abuse, alcoholic parent, and loss of a loved one. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had great closure with a jump ahead epilogue and a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I paid $3.79 on Amazon for it back in 2014.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This should be <u>Safe</u> for the safety gals.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have the H pushing the h away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a ~6 week separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse (but mentions that H was abused by parents as a child - no flashbacks)<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_243258401" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/243258401" />
    <a title="Baba  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669232-baba"><img alt="Baba  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564910043p2/4669232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/243258401?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Baba  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Baba  " href="/user/show/4669232-baba">Baba  </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=memorable-favorite-heroes">memorable-favorite-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=memorable-favorite-heroines">memorable-favorite-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=books-kelly-and-baba-liked-or-loved">books-kelly-and-baba-liked-or-loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=five-star-reads">five-star-reads</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer243258401" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10611232227631933616">Edited May 30, 2012 (original review December 2011)<br/><br/><b>"Luck is believing you're lucky."<br/>- by Tennessee Williams -<br/><br/>"Life is the first gift, love the second, and understanding the third."<br/>- by Marge Piercy -</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/?action=view&current=tattoos-for-men.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379774437i/329421._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Nothing beats my Tate Jackson and Sweet Dreams, but I can truly say that I loved Lady Luck too!<br/><br/><br/><i>Very brief synopsis:</i><br/>Ty Walker is half-black. He won a poker game and someone got pissed and wanted to punish him. Ty was set up and took the fall for someone else and therefore was wrongly imprisoned. W</span>
  <span id="freeText10611232227631933616" style="display:none">Edited May 30, 2012 (original review December 2011)<br><br><b>"Luck is believing you're lucky."<br>- by Tennessee Williams -<br><br>"Life is the first gift, love the second, and understanding the third."<br>- by Marge Piercy -</b><br><br><a href="http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/?action=view&amp;current=tattoos-for-men.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379774437i/329421._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Nothing beats my Tate Jackson and Sweet Dreams, but I can truly say that I loved Lady Luck too!<br><br><br><i>Very brief synopsis:</i><br>Ty Walker is half-black. He won a poker game and someone got pissed and wanted to punish him. Ty was set up and took the fall for someone else and therefore was wrongly imprisoned. When he's released he walks straight to Lexie Berry. 'Shift' owes Ty. Shift is also a former friend of Ronnie. Ronnie was Lexie's boyfriend, and he got killed four years ago. Shift tells Lexie to pick Ty up. Unfortunately he didn't tell Lexie that Ty intends to marry her in Vegas. Ty needs her to put a plan into action. His revenge. <br><br>***********************************************************************<br><br>In the beginning of the story Ty is rather crude, rude, and very taciturn. Others may not understand it, however I had no problem with his being and acting like that. He comes out of a penitentiary for a crime he didn't commit. I don't think that everyone would feel totally grateful and happy to the world after being wrongly imprisoned. Ty is not bitter but he is really angry and he has trust issues. He seeks revenge.<br><br>Ty had a shitty childhood and growing up the way he did, dreams he had died early. He had to learn not to hope for too much when he experienced the bitter taste of disappointment. While the story unfolds, the asshole Ty was long gone and the taciturn Ty was a faded memory. Ty doesn't talk very much but at least he shares and he listens. Ty is a hot and intense alpha male who makes your toes curl. Yum! Besides his super hot body and incredibly good looks, he is in fact a generous, gentle, thoughtful, and protective man. I really loved him, maybe not during the first few chapters…But I felt for him and I think I did understand him.<br><br>Lexie…wow, another wonderful heroine…I admired the fun lovin' Lexie. Boy, does she like to "throw sass" (Ty's words). She had a very hard childhood and it's amazing to see that this person grew up to become such a fine, determined, and strong woman. She made a home for Ty and herself. She helped him by being herself. She was there for him and she gave as good as she got. And she made him smile and laugh. Lexie feels the vibes of friendship through Ty's friends. She needed that badly and she thinks it's a good and clean feeling. It feels right.<br><br><i>A shout out to Jill</i><br>About this mama nickname. After my initial WTF moment I really got used to it. It's kind of sweet and endearing. And if the shoe fits, wear it!!! I hope you'll get a feeling when you're reading the "quotes". I was wondering why he did call her mama. There could be a few reasons. His childhood and his mom were far from being perfect. Lexie made a home for him, she pampered him. She did things a mom would do for her child. Lexie calls him hubby and he replied by saying she's a goof and he calls her mama. Hubby and mama, that's quite a combo. Actually, Ty calls her "babe" and "baby" too…<br><br>When I was about 57 % into the story I almost (almost) had to endure a heart attack. Yeah, yeah, Ty, Lexie 'played' you, but since she did it for your own f***in' good, you should have been grateful!!! You said nasty things and acted like a dumb jerk! I am so glad you realized your mistake and you redeemed yourself. Again. *wipes eyebrows*<br><br>I admire the author's ability to create so much intimacy, lots of intimacy, actually. I don't necessarily mean the sex; it is much more about a look, a touch, a movement, a word. I hope you know what I mean. There's a lot of touching and she describes what Ty's doing with his hands; that's part of the intimacy. Or they're standing in the kitchen and he's eating. The whole process of describing that IS intimacy.<br>The author does such a fine job in developing the characters through lots of emotions. The pace is very good - again - and since the book is so long, there is never a need to rush things. It grows steadily. We really get to know the main couple and so many complex and interesting secondary characters as well. I loved the dialogs and I really appreciated to meet so many wonderful secondary characters. The plot is good and I just love Ms. Ashley's detailed and colorful writing! As usual there's a lot of swearing (f and s-bomb) but it fits the characters.<br><br>A reader mentioned that she didn't like the racist conflict of the story. I disagree and I even appreciated that part. I'm glad there are author's who show the readers that racism is present. I know whereof I speak. My two boys are half-black and they are confronted with racial problems. Big problems start out small, and I know it is substantial to cope with minor problems before they grow and will really cause harm.<br><br><br><b>I put my memorable "quotes"/lines in a spoiler. You may read them though, since I didn't include any spoilers. Enjoy!</b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[&lt;…&gt;It was an arms crushing me to his body, heads slanting, mouths opened, tongues invading, toes curling, knees weakening, bones dissolving, deep, wet, hungry, carnal kiss. It seemed to last forever but that forever was not near long enough.&lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;"You're part-goof all class. Never walked in a room, any room, with a woman on my arm, any woman, who's got your looks, your style, the kinda beauty you got and the light that shines from you. So I don't get it. I don't get how a woman leads a life full of shit and comes out of it bein' part-goof and all class. That shit's impossible but there you fuckin' are. Part-goof, all class."<br>I felt my breath coming fast but managed to whisper, "I'm not part-goof."<br>"You're right. I was bein' nice. You're a total goof."<br>"Am not"<br>"Babe, you call me 'hubby'," he pointed out but my breath came faster because he called me "babe" again.<br>"You are my hubby."<br>"No one says hubby," he told me.<br>"I do," I told him.<br>"All right, I'll rephrase. No one but a goof says hubby."….&lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;Days before, seconds after she told him she wanted to have breakfast with her husband and he liked hearing her say that, he liked it too fucking much, he fucked up. Then he kept fucking up. Then he kept fucking doing it. He knew it and he couldn't stop.<br>Then, the instant she pressed her mouth to his, her soft body in his lap, overwhelmed with emotion and sharing that with him he lost control and he knew he couldn't do that. And the only way he could manage to keep control was to stay the fuck away from her, her sweet smiles, her soft voice, her brightness, that fantastic fucking body. He couldn't hold up. So he stayed the fuck away from her and spent a lot of time thinking about how to encourage her to stay the fuck away from him.&lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;"No, Ty, you drew it when one second you had your tongue in my mouth, your hands on me and me on my back in your bed and swear to God, swear to God, that was all you had to do, I was this close," she lifted a hand and held her thumb and forefinger an inch apart, "to climax just with that and the next second you took it all away from me. All of it and you fucking know exactly what I'm talking about because the next second I was standing on my feet, you were two feet away but you might as well still have been in fucking California and then I watched you shut down."&lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;….That's how he made his living. He gave me a pen and ink. This," he lifted his left arm then dropped it back to the bed. "After he died, I had it inked on me. Took what he gave me to a tattoo parlor right after the funeral and got it started."<br>Her voice held a tone of light dawning as she whispered, "So he was your Ella."<br>Her light dawned clear for her and for Walker because she was right.<br>"Yeah, he was my Ella."<br>"So it was Tuku who brought out my Ty."<br>My Ty.<br>My Ty.<br>Christ. Fuck.<br>Christ.<br>Two words. Just two words. Walker had no clue until that moment that two words could mean so fucking much. He'd never belonged to anyone. He'd never belonged anywhere. Never thought he wanted to.<br>Until he heard those two words.<br>He couldn't keep the thick out of his voice when he confirmed, "Yeah, it was him."&lt;…&gt;<br><br>Tate and Ty:<br>&lt;…&gt;"Man, we've been married less than a month," Walker reminded him.<br>"So?"<br>Walker stared at him.<br>Then he muttered, "Fuck me, Tatum Jackson, family man and advocate for domestic bliss."<br>"You been busy with your woman, not around, you been around me, Laurie and Jonas, you'd see I got it goin' on," Tate told him through a grin.<br>"Fuck me," Walker muttered again.<br>Jackson kept grinning at him.<br>Then the grin faded and he whispered, "Think about it. And call me with a night you can come over."<br>"Right," Walker murmured.&lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;When I was done speaking I felt his body had gone still again, stone still.<br>And silent.<br>Then he asked quietly, "Nightmare?"<br>"Nightmare," I replied firmly.<br>Ty didn't move.<br>By a miracle, I held it together.<br>Then he moved but it was to rest his chin on my shoulder and I closed my eyes because I needed him to go, go, go so I could fall apart again on my own.<br>Then he said, "Your nightmare, mama, was my dream."<br>My heart clenched.<br>He kept going. "Never had a home until you gave me one."<br>My breath started sticking.<br>"Never had anyone give to me the way you gave to me."<br>My breath stopped sticking and clogged.<br>"Never thought of findin' a woman who I wanted to have my baby."<br>Oh God.<br>"Never had light in my life, never, not once, I lived wild but I didn't burn bright until you shined your light on me."<br>Oh God.<br>"Whacked, fuckin' insane, but, at night, you curled in front of me, didn't mind I did that time that wasn't mine 'cause it meant I walked out to you."<br>He had to stop. He had to.<br>He didn't.<br>"Your nightmare," he whispered, turned his head and against my neck he finished, "my dream."&lt;…&gt;<br><br><br>You can laugh as much as you want but I do love it when he calls her mama - so sweet and endearing! If the shoe fits, wear it!<br><br>&lt;…&gt;His body shook as his grin spread to a smile. Then he asked, "You honestly think you can tackle me?"<br>"I didn't say it would be a successful tackle."<br>And then my husband burst out laughing.<br>And I watched.<br>He didn't give this to me often but I always watched. This time it was way better because he was doing it while still inside me.<br>Then his laughter died to a chuckle, he dropped his forehead to mine and his hand came up and curled around the side of my neck.<br>And when he did the last, the laughter died, his eyes held mine and he whispered, "Is my mama home?"<br>I swallowed but I still knew my eyes got bright and my voice was husky when I whispered back, "Yes."<br>He closed his eyes, shifted the lower half of his face and touched his mouth to mine. Then he lifted his head away, opened his eyes and I felt his thumb stroke my jaw.<br>His gaze again locked with mine, he told me gently, "Missed you, baby."<br>I swallowed again and my arms and legs tightened around him. "Me too."&lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;Then he dropped his head and kept going slow, but, lips to her ear, he asked, "How many you want?"<br>"Four," she answered immediately and he quit moving, luckily on an inward glide and his head came up.<br>"Four?" he asked.<br>"Four," Lexie answered.<br>"Four kids?" he added detail in order to confirm.<br>She grinned again. "Four kids."<br>"Shit, mama, good thing we're gettin' started tomorrow."&lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;Therefore he asked quietly, "Remember I told you about Tuku?" Julius nodded. Ty went on, "Got good friends, a lot of them, feel deep for them all. Only three people in my life got more from me, one of 'em's in the ground, one of 'em's sitting' on the deck and the last is standin' right in front of me."<br>Julius said not a word but held his eyes.<br>Then Ty whispered, "Gratitude, brother."<br>Julius kept his eyes locked with Ty's and whispered back, "Debt paid."&lt;…&gt;<br><br>Another one…*snickers*<br><br>&lt;…&gt;So I bought Ty and I black tees that said on the front, "Team Walker" in big white letters and in smaller lettered italics with quotes under it, "We never admit defeat". On the back of Ty's it said, "Mr. Humongo" and on the back of mine it said, "Mr. Humongo's Mama".<br>I freaking loved them.<br>Ty would take one look at them and think I was a total goof.&lt;…&gt;<br><br>I mentioned that Lexie likes to "throw sass". An example:<br>&lt;…&gt;"Go home," I ordered and went on without giving either of them an opening. "And don't come back. I don't know you but I do know you taught your son to make certain he took his dirty dishes to the sink by throwing a glass at him and giving him a scar. Ty's lucky, he's hot and that scar, admittedly, makes him hotter but he's not lucky he's got a mother who'd risk blinding her son in one eye because she's a lunatic with a bad attitude who would throw a glass at a nine year old child and then, years later, after he endured a nightmare, not appear at his door with open arms and a welcome home bouquet but months later show up at his house for the sole purpose of behaving like a bitter shrew and expressing her whacked opinion that she thinks her son owes her shit. My husband does not owe you shit, he does not owe giving you what he's worked hard to earn, he does not owe you his time, he does not owe you one fucking thing. Now go home and do not come back."&lt;…&gt;<br><br>Now this made me go all awwwwwwww!!! (it's even longer, I just had to cut it…)<br>&lt;…&gt;Tate fell silent.<br>Ty didn't.<br>"Since the day I was released, you knocked yourself out. You had my back, you took care of Lexie when we had our thing then you did what you could to help me sort that. It's important to me that you know I'm grateful. I've been tryin' to figure out how I can show how much but, keep thinkin' on it, nothin' comes to mind and I know why. I get it. You're a man who has everything so there is nothing I can hand you that you want or need. And I get that because I am now that same man. So the only thing I can give you are words and, my guess is, that'll be enough. If it isn't, you name it and it's yours."<br>"Friends do what I did for friends," Tate returned.<br>"No they don't, Tate. You did what you did for me because you're you. That's what I'm talkin' about."<br>Tate ws silent a moment then he said, "Well then, you guessed right. Words are enough."<br>Ty nodded.<br>Tate tipped his head to the side and asked jokingly, "We done with the near-midnight in the middle of fuckin' nowhere heart-to-heart?"<br>Ty didn't feel like joking and answered, "No."<br>"Then what -?"<br>"Love you, man," Ty interrupted quietly.<br>"Learned the hard way not to delay in expressing that sentiment so I'm not gonna delay. You call me brother and I got one who's blood who don't mean shit to me and today, all this shit done, rejoicing and reflecting, it hit me that I got two who aren't blood but who do mean something. And you're one of those two."<br>"Ty-" Tate murmured.<br>"I will never forget, until I die, what you did for me and my wife and until that day I will never stop bein' grateful."<br>"Fuck man," Tate whispered.<br>"Now, do those words work so you get what you did mean to me?"<br>Silence then, "Yeah, they work."<br>"Good, then now we're done with our near-midnight, middle of fuckin' nowhere heart-to-heart," Ty declared, turned, opened the door to the Viper and started folding in.<br>He stopped with his ass nearly to the seat and looked up over the door when Tate called his name.<br>"I don't have a blood brother," Tate said. "But you should know there's a reason I call you that."&lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;"Lady Luck finally saw fit to shine her light on me but life taught me to share. Welcome to the light."&lt;…&gt;<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Lady Luck may start out a little bit bumpy but it got better and better. Ty was a difficult character in the beginning of the story but he proved himself, and I became familiar with him. I really loved this guy! Ms. Ashley is able to create super hot alpha male heroes who will make your toes curl and really sassy heroines who can hold their own. The last few chapters are intense and thrilling and the story is nicely wrapped up with a very beautiful and hilarious epilogue. Lady Luck is another engaging and wonderful story written by an author I truly admire! Anyone who loves her books should give Lady Luck a go. Enjoy!<br><br>I am so looking forward to reading book 4 (Chace and Faye's story)! I can't wait to get my hands on their book!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer260589980" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7133360865894871133"><b>Huge 5+ stars</b> <br/><br/>Wow! What a fantastic story! <i>Lady Luck</i> was a book I was leery to read. I knew I would struggle with the hero, knowing how crass and disrespectful toward women he was, and I was right. What I didn't expect, however, was that I would ended up not only loving this passionate, emotional, intense, and captivating story, but I would also fall head-over-heels in love with the hero. <br/><br/>There were many things I loved about this book, but it was the love story between the hero and heroine, Ty a</span>
  <span id="freeText7133360865894871133" style="display:none"><b>Huge 5+ stars</b> <br /><br />Wow! What a fantastic story! <i>Lady Luck</i> was a book I was leery to read. I knew I would struggle with the hero, knowing how crass and disrespectful toward women he was, and I was right. What I didn't expect, however, was that I would ended up not only loving this passionate, emotional, intense, and captivating story, but I would also fall head-over-heels in love with the hero. <br /><br />There were many things I loved about this book, but it was the love story between the hero and heroine, Ty and Lexie, that stole my heart and captured my imagination. I truly love this couple. The romance between Ty and Lexie was powerful and full of  devotion, admiration, understanding, tenderness, acceptance, and steamy hot passion. Of all the Kristen Ashley books I've read, Ty and Lexie's relationship felt the most authentic and substantial. They easily became one of my all time favorite couples, and Lexie by far my favorite heroine to date. <br /><br /><i>Lady Luck</i> is another amazing story by Kristen Ashley. It's definitely a favorite! <br /><br /><i>If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</i></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_1569109082" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1569109082" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1569109082?book_show_action=true">Mar 04, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=buddy-read-with-bbbs">buddy-read-with-bbbs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1569109082" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3927225913217121417">Every weekend I join the cool-girls in the BBB group and read a Kristen Ashley book with them. And, every weekend, I rant about how the alpha-males are complete assholes. It's a tradition that I enjoy - like the tradition of dying Easter eggs. Sure, you have to deal with the smell of boiled eggs and vinegar, the mess of little cups of dye all over the table that never seems to come off, and the annoyance of trying to figure out something to do with all of those dyed eggs later (blue and pink egg</span>
  <span id="freeText3927225913217121417" style="display:none">Every weekend I join the cool-girls in the BBB group and read a Kristen Ashley book with them. And, every weekend, I rant about how the alpha-males are complete assholes. It's a tradition that I enjoy - like the tradition of dying Easter eggs. Sure, you have to deal with the smell of boiled eggs and vinegar, the mess of little cups of dye all over the table that never seems to come off, and the annoyance of trying to figure out something to do with all of those dyed eggs later (blue and pink egg salad anyone?), but you'd never consider skipping it because of the fun you have with your fellow egg-dyers. The BBB girls are my fellow egg-dyers, so bring on the stinky mess!<br><br>See, Kristen Ashley books have a formula: <br><br>a total caveman alpha whose behavior borders on abuse and at times even criminal<br><br>a female who is skittish about being involved with this man for various reasons (none of them being that he is a pushy asshole for some reason. More like '<i>I'm not pretty enough for him</i>' *eye roll*)<br><br>a crime that is complicated and directly involves the couple<br><br>at least one kidnapping - possibly more<br><br>a gay guy<br><br>a zany character who steals the show<br><br>at least one break-up <br><br>and tons of interruptions and misunderstandings between the couple.<br><br>These things are in every book. If you haven't had a kidnapping yet, it's coming. It's always coming.<br><br>So, in this book we have Ty, a guy who is getting out of prison after serving 5 years for a crime he didn't commit; and Lexie, a girl who picks him up from prison as a favor to her ex-boyfriend's friend. Ty has spent his 5 years in prison plotting revenge on the people who set him up. He needs a wife who will be his alibi and have his back if the bad guys try to frame him again. He offers Lexie 50 grand to play wife to him. She is no fool and agrees.<br><br>Of course they fall in love. We have learned that these kind of situations always turn out that way <i>in books and movies</i>.<br><br>The book was fun and action filled. Lexie and Ty were a very cute couple. And, here's the thing - I actually liked Ty! He is the first guy in this series that I have actually liked. Except, one big thing: he has a mouth on him that is so crude that I wanted to smack him. I get that he was in prison, but come on! That was my only problem with this guy, though, and that's saying a lot for a KA book. If we could take all of the times he uses those horrible words for women and replace them with "ladies", "girls", "gals", or even "females", I would have been a happy camper.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457241215i/18337431.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>That's right, gay man. You know how to treat a lady!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3927225913217121417" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer716550343" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7896844883604347010">Thoughts after a re read.<br/><br/>Still a 5 star read for me.<br/><br/>I love how Ty "enters" the story. The first time we "see" him. <br/><br/><b>
  <i> I glanced at my watch to see it was twelve oh seven and then I glanced down the tunnel again and something was moving though the shimmers. That path was long and the heat on the day was immense so I didn't see much but something made me keep watching.<br/><br/>And as the thing moving through the shimmers formed into a man, I kept watching as my breath started sticking in my throat.<br/><br/>Then th</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText7896844883604347010" style="display:none">Thoughts after a re read.<br /><br />Still a 5 star read for me.<br /><br />I love how Ty "enters" the story. The first time we "see" him. <br /><br /><b>
  <i> I glanced at my watch to see it was twelve oh seven and then I glanced down the tunnel again and something was moving though the shimmers. That path was long and the heat on the day was immense so I didn't see much but something made me keep watching.<br /><br />And as the thing moving through the shimmers formed into a man, I kept watching as my breath started sticking in my throat.<br /><br />Then the man kept getting closer, coming into focus through the heat waves and my breath grew shallow as my body grew still.<br /><br />I didn't blink. I didn't move. I just watched that man coming at me and my car.<br /><br />Then he got even closer and my body moved for me. I didn't have to tell it to move, it just did. Without taking my eyes off him, my hand reached for the door handle, released it and I unfolded out of the car, losing sight of him only when the roof was in my way for less then a second.<br /><br />...<br /><br />He was huge. Huge. I'd never seen a man that big. He had to be six foot five, six foot six, maybe even taller.<br /><br />His shoulders were immensely broad. The wall of his chest was just that. A wall. His hips were narrow, his thighs enormous. He was muscle from neck down, pure, firm, defined, muscle.<br /><br />........<br /><br />That said, his face, though sheer male beauty, was blank. Scary blank Expressionless. Completely. His eyes were on me standing in my opened door watching him round the hood and turning with his movements. But there was nothing in those eyes. Nothing. Void.<br /><br />It was terrifying</i>
</b><br /><br />Awesome and breath taking, I could almost feel the heat as I was reading, and quite frankly, it just got better.<br /><br />This is a beautiful story of two people, who have repeatedly had shit handed to them in life, coming together, when neither expected it and finding something beautiful, but too scared to to trust it at times. Brilliant 5 stars.</span>

    <a title="Shawna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1802746-shawna"><img alt="Shawna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574172018p2/1802746.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/258093952?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shawna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shawna" href="/user/show/1802746-shawna">Shawna</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of emotional contemporary romance, lovable heroines, &amp; hot alpha heroes</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>,
