        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer258093952" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3424086880384586241">5+ stars – Contemporary Romance<br/><br/>A bunch of my fellow romance lovin’ Goodreads friends have been reading and raving about Kristen Ashley, and with great reason. <b>
  <i>Lady Luck</i>
</b> is the third book in the <i>Colorado Mountain</i> series, and after reading it, I’m now 3 for 3 with her books being big 5 star winners that I <i>loved</i>.<br/><br/>There’s just something about her stories that grab me right from the beginning and never let go. I especially love how the details, descriptions, and conversations depict such vivid ima</span>
  <span id="freeText3424086880384586241" style="display:none">5+ stars – Contemporary Romance<br><br>A bunch of my fellow romance lovin’ Goodreads friends have been reading and raving about Kristen Ashley, and with great reason. <b>
  <i>Lady Luck</i>
</b> is the third book in the <i>Colorado Mountain</i> series, and after reading it, I’m now 3 for 3 with her books being big 5 star winners that I <i>loved</i>.<br><br>There’s just something about her stories that grab me right from the beginning and never let go. I especially love how the details, descriptions, and conversations depict such vivid images of the characters and scenes so that it feels like you’re watching a movie in your mind. It’s true that the editing could use improvement and there’s perhaps <i>too</i> much elucidation of inane minutiae, like clothes, jewelry, outfits, rooms, furniture, and common “stuff”. But overall Ashley’s unique writing style and genuine, engaging dialogue bring the story and cast to life. Her books are unusually lengthy and take me longer to read than other authors/books, but then astonishingly when they’re over, I’m sad and still want more. Fortunately, she also gives her readers superb epilogues that more than satisfy.<br><br>I absolutely adored Lexie, but I didn’t warm up to Ty quite as easily. I felt bad for him and all that he endured, and his anger, cynical mistrust of women, and desire for vengeance were more than justified. Even so, Ty’s cruel treatment of Lexie in a couple of momentous, heartbreakingly intense scenes really pissed me off. I cried like a baby and felt nearly as emotionally flayed and raw afterward as she did. Lexie’s such an incredibly sweet, loyal, giving, and loving heroine, and I wasn’t sure he’d be able to win <i>me</i> back after he’d hurt her so terribly and unforgivably. Amazingly he did, and with icing and a cherry on top. It certainly didn’t hurt that he’s a smokin’ hot, tortured, badass alpha, which I can never resist. <br><br>Crude language doesn’t bother me, but there’s <i>a lot</i> of fuckin’, pussy, and bitch talk in this that got somewhat grating at times. Also, I didn’t really care for Ty’s nickname “mama” for Lexie initially, but it grew on me after a while.<br><br>My summary of the <i>Colorado Mountain</i> series so far:<br>Favorite hero: Max from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11227041.The_Gamble__Colorado_Mountain___1_" title="The Gamble (Colorado Mountain, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">The Gamble</a><br>Favorite heroine: Lexie from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12958487.Lady_Luck__Colorado_Mountain___3_" title="Lady Luck (Colorado Mountain, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Luck</a><br>Favorite overall story/book: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11227040.Sweet_Dreams__Colorado_Mountain___2_" title="Sweet Dreams (Colorado Mountain, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Dreams</a> <br>And I can’t wait for Chace and Faye’s story! <br><br>I’m glad she’s got an extensive backlist and more book releases coming because I definitely want to read more by this author! Big 5 stars!<br><br>I envisioned hunkalicious Boris Kodjoe as Ty. He doesn’t have enough tats, but I’ve got a great imagination and could mentally tat him up. <br><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=BdayBorisKodjoe.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379768612i/269685._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=boris-kodjoe.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380366743i/719078._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=ttta.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380366743i/719079.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=BorisKodjoe-main-twitter.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379766661i/248932.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

I think either of them could play her with the perfect mix of sweet, goof, and sass.<br><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=jennifer-garner-choc-0610-de.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer13634835594090144281">As much as I hated Motorcycle Man, I *still* thought that maybe I was missing something. Did I pick the wrong book? Will I find the magic with another?<br/>The answer is no. <br/><br/>*I've edited this dang thing so many times and it never sounds exactly right to me so bullet points it is. Blerg.<br/><br/>-Race/Racism as a plot device. The same drama/conflicts of every other KA book are present here (evul women, kidnapping) except this time cuz racism. Badly executed, ham-fisted, cartoonish, just...no. I don't need this</span>
  <span id="freeText13634835594090144281" style="display:none">As much as I hated Motorcycle Man, I *still* thought that maybe I was missing something. Did I pick the wrong book? Will I find the magic with another?<br />The answer is no. <br /><br />*I've edited this dang thing so many times and it never sounds exactly right to me so bullet points it is. Blerg.<br /><br />-Race/Racism as a plot device. The same drama/conflicts of every other KA book are present here (evul women, kidnapping) except this time cuz racism. Badly executed, ham-fisted, cartoonish, just...no. I don't need this author to paint a very heavy, serious topic with her OTT brush. It's offensive and she gets no props for it. She gets away with a lot that black authors would get severely criticized for, IMO. <br /><br />-"Just to explain and update a few things…" is used to transition scenes. I can't.<br /><br />-99% of the action happens on the phone. Ty makes NO MOVES. What a hero!<br /><br />-Hero talks in Caveman Pidgin. Occasionally he talks in Overgrown Toddler. At one point Ty said to Lexie, "Mama. Kiss." NOT SEXY. NOT CUTE. Apparently every KA hero talks this way. What the actual fuck?<br /><br />-Over-descriptiveness of things that no one could give a fuck about: "her other hand going into her hair at her forehead, pulling the thick, shining, waving dark mass back, lifting a huge bunch of it at the back of her head and shaking it a couple of times before dropping it only for it to fall into and around her face again, settling on her shoulders and streaming down her back." It would have been nice if the action and suspense of the story were given this sort of detail. Nah, let's waste time talking about hair and sunken kitchens and smothered pork chops. -_-<br /><br />-Sex scenes suck.<br /><br />In conclusion, NOPE!</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_255326398" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/255326398" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/255326398?book_show_action=true">Jan 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer255326398" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18383599132169762240"><b> <i> "We'd weathered one hell of a storm. But we didn't come out with nicks and dents. We came out tougher, stronger, closer." </i> </b><br/><br/>*GRIN* Squee!! Another winner from Kristen Ashley :D<br/><br/>I seriously <i> cannot </i> get enough of her books!! I'm totally,utterly, blissfully <i> ADDICTED </i>!!!!<br/><br/>Ty Walker just got released from prison. Lexie owes a guy so she agreed to pick him up and get him to wherever he needed to go, thinking it would be a quick and easy task. But Ty has enemies, and she's with Ty, she needs his prote</span>
  <span id="freeText18383599132169762240" style="display:none"><b> <i> "We'd weathered one hell of a storm. But we didn't come out with nicks and dents. We came out tougher, stronger, closer." </i> </b><br><br>*GRIN* Squee!! Another winner from Kristen Ashley :D<br><br>I seriously <i> cannot </i> get enough of her books!! I'm totally,utterly, blissfully <i> ADDICTED </i>!!!!<br><br>Ty Walker just got released from prison. Lexie owes a guy so she agreed to pick him up and get him to wherever he needed to go, thinking it would be a quick and easy task. But Ty has enemies, and she's with Ty, she needs his protection, he needs someone at his back, and he works out a deal with her to marry him until he does what he needs to do and once its done, they'll go their separate ways. But what she thought would be a simple pick up, turned out to be a crazy roller-coaster filled with corrupt police departments, road trips, over-achieving pimps, racist dirty cops, vengence, betrayals, undercover agents, and in the middle of all this maddness, finding crazy, intense, passionate love that sweeps them both off their feet.<br><br>I literally loved Ty right from the beginning. He was very different from a lot of KA's other male characters in the he was fairly non-verbal. He didn't say a lot but when he spoke, his words had weight.<br><br>He knows what he wants, and he was willing to work as hard as was necessary to get it. And right off the bat, he wanted Lexie. Like now.<br><br>But I just loved how smart and nearly always in control of himself he was. He was also driven, and not one to be tempted away from his goals by stupidity.<br><br>Lexie was an amazing heroine. Maybe even one of my fav KA ones so far. She was very much like a female Brock (from Dream Man #2). She was sassy, but very deeply understanding. She was fun-loving, but very open, honest, caring, and fair. She was straight to the point and didn't bullshit her way through anything. And, lol, she was a bit of a goof :P<br><br>I loved Ty and Lexie's "give and take" way of getting to know each other. Just like their relationship, it was fair, open and funtional... as well as being a great way to learn about each other.<br><br>We got a really cool deviation from the KA norm in this book in that the whole story was told in alternating POV's between Ty and Lexie. This was amazing for so many reasons. Firstly, we got to see (long term) inside the head of a KA man - got to experience him seeing Lexie "throwing sass" and thinking it was cute, got to be on the other side of the banter...<br><br><i> "He looked to her and saw her shove an entire Ding Dong in her mouth.<br>Ding Dongs.<br>Christ.<br>Total goof.<br>They hit the highway, she jacked the music up and he experienced the unusual desire to beg someone to drive ice picks into his ears so he wouldn't have to listen to it." </i><br><br>And secondly, his POV was great because, since he wasn't a very verbal guy, it was really great to be able to understand where he was coming from, why he did the things he did, what he experienced during fights, and even several smokin' HOT love scenes from his POV.<br><br>There were times when the story made my head spin with the complexity of the plot line (for which I knocked off the .5 star) but that was my only complaint... and it doesn't overpower the story. In fact, we actually get to see a LOT of Ty and Lexie as a couple in this book.<br><br><b> <i> "Never had a light in my life, never, not once. I lived wild but I didn't burn bright until you shined your light on me." </i> </b><br><br>There is a huge focus on their actual relationship in Lady Luck and I love that we got to see them as a fully functional couple for a good chunk of the story. They have nearly instant attraction for each other and start their connection quite early on. Sure, there are a few bumps in the road (one in particular that put my heart right in my throat!) but they get over them fast and learn from their mistakes and only end up closer as a result of them.<br><br><b> <i> "This is it, Team Walker, you and me. We want somethin', we find a way to get it. We hit a rough patch, we find a way to get over it. We face a challenge, we find a way to beat it. It's good, we savor it. What I'm sayin' is, this team is a winner. We never forget to celebrate the victories and we get a lotta those because we never admit defeat." </i> </b><br><br>I also really loved that even though the story (what with uncovering the truth behind Ty's wrongful conviction) had a whole lot of drama, within their relationship, they were pretty solid. And even when they did screw up, the reason behind the screw up was always completely understandable - never stupid or out-of-the-blue. And they both knew how to apologize, and apologize well... lol, you'll all know that this made me a very happy reader :P<br><br>And boy were their (frequent) sexy times H.O.T.!!! I mean <i> really HOT! </i> I fanned my way through many a bedroom scene.<br><br>Another thing that fans of Sweet Dreams (book #2) will love is how much of Tate we get to see in this book!! He's one of Ty's two best friends and we see a lot of him (and Laurie). Definitely made for some squee-worthy moments! (Although, we didn't really see much more than a fleeting glimpse of Max unfortunately. I'm looking forward to the next book because I hear he's more heavily featured in it... YAY! I miss him!)<br><br><i> "He had good friends. The kind of friends you didn't just get. The kind of friends you earned." </i><br><br>And I also thought it was so cool that we were introduced to Chase, the hero of the next book, about half way though this one. He's not a feature character, but he's there a lot and I really liked getting to know him a little and see a bit of his back story from afar before reading his book.<br><br>The epilogue was fantastic and it was LONG! What a treat! KA's epilogues always leave me grinning and with the best feelings... there is something so comforting about seeing the characters you have come to know and love get their HEAs in detail. So heart warming!! &lt;3<br><br>4.5+ stars<br><br>Here's how I see Ty and Lexie:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380754305i/3119885._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="18383599132169762240" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer313336193" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11837923050842171726">My favorite Colorado <3 This is a beautiful story, even if it's about revenge and rasizm, KA really knows how to write them.<br/><br/>10 stars from me :)))<br/><br/>The writing - I don't usually comment on KA-s writing style, I know a lot of people don't like it, concerning the grammar and stuff, but I'm not one of them. When I read I read emotions, and KA novels have that, and it's pictured perfectly. I mean, like in this one, when we read from TY-s point of view, every freaking time he got that thing that pierced</span>
  <span id="freeText11837923050842171726" style="display:none">My favorite Colorado &lt;3 This is a beautiful story, even if it's about revenge and rasizm, KA really knows how to write them.<br /><br />10 stars from me :)))<br /><br />The writing - I don't usually comment on KA-s writing style, I know a lot of people don't like it, concerning the grammar and stuff, but I'm not one of them. When I read I read emotions, and KA novels have that, and it's pictured perfectly. I mean, like in this one, when we read from TY-s point of view, every freaking time he got that thing that pierced through his chest on the left side, I swear I felt it too. I just can't read that and not get into it. And in the middle of the novel there's a chapter in which she says something bad's gonna happen, and I was in stomach chramps when thad bad thing actually happened, she really knows how to build the tension, I was on needles, and it was my second read. I remember my first, man that was tough. <br /><br /><i> He looked in her blue-gray eyes and there it was. Or, more to the point, there it wasn’t.<br /><br />The light was out. </i><br /><br />That's what I mean, I know what happened, and when he saw the lights were out, my throat just closed.<br />So for me, KA writing has quality, if I can smile, laugh, cry, get misty-eyed, annoyed and angsty - that's all I can ask for :)<br /><br />The story - It's about revenge, rasizm and dirty cops. Now, this doesn't sound very appealing, a bit of a heavy subject, but I loved it, and KA wrote it so well &lt;3 Just great :) Ty was set up, he ended in prison for 5 years, now that he's out he wants revenge for the time he lost. Lexie is forced to do a favor for a shady guy who does dirty business, she picks up Ty when he gets out of jail, the go to Vegas and get married XD <br /><br />Lexie - She's had a really tough time in her life, been with a pimp and a drug dealer who got shot. Then she does a favor for another pimp/drug dealer, mostly because she can't get out of that life without some help. That's why she accepts Ty's offer, they get married, he gives her money and helps her start a new life. Of course, Ty being the most beautiful man she ever saw, and the sparks flying all over, that fake marriage was doomed from the start to become a real one :))<br /><br />Ty - KA doesn't do much of tortured heroes, but Ty here would mostly fit that description :) He's been decieved by a woman, the town police framed him for a crime he didn't commit, he was in jail for 5 years and wants revenge. He of course has a lot of issues, one being not to trust any "pussy" as he refers it XD the second are his jail demons which he has a hard time getting over. But Lex is something different, he sees that from the start, they bond pretty fast, that scene in Vegas when he gets to the pool and she smiles at him - swoony to the max &lt;3 He made some stupid desisions, part from fear of being betrayed, part from anger from being played, even if it was for his own good :P All in all he is a complex character, and really does it for me, just love him :)<br /><br />Favorite scenes<br />- the non-verb conversation in the diner after he gets out XDXD<br />- at the pool when she smiles at him<br />- when she makes the glass thingy from the bouquet<br />- when he finds her at the beach :((( man I cried at that one<br />- when she sees him alive in the house<br /><br /><br />BTW, in this one we got a glimpse of Chase and Faye &lt;3 Can't wait to read them :))))</span>

  <span id="freeText4680314544594758615" style="display:none"><b>5/5</b><br><br><b>reread:</b> <br>26/05/17<br>10/11/17<br>01/01/19<br>03/05/19 <br>24/11/20 <br><br><i>Holy hell I forgot how much I loved the little endearments and plots-twists in this one. If I am ever in need of a crazy romance fix <i>(which is all the time and I ain't ashamed about nothing)</i>, Kristen is my go-to girl. <br><br>Her books are outrageous with borderline ridiculous plots, filled to the brim with alpha males and women who can give it as good as they get it. And <b>angst.</b> So much entertaining angst that leaves you in tears. <br><br>Lexie Berry meets Ty Walker for the first time when she picks him up from jail, where he had served five years for a murder he didn't commit, framed because he was bi-racial and came from a town where the cops didn't like anybody with colour. <br><br>Together they go back to Ty's home town, where they strike a deal that helps both of them. They are the most adorable characters who bicker like crazy and are full of drama. Probably my favourite in this series, the side characters that come along with them are well-fleshed and hilarious. Couldn't get enough and I'm thinking about this book days after. <br><br>I'm not telling you more because I don't want to ruin all the feels. <div id="review_1057749077" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1057749077" />
    <a title="Choko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27962805-choko"><img alt="Choko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475642755p2/27962805.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1057749077?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Choko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Choko" href="/user/show/27962805-choko">Choko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1057749077" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12314166507452318553"><b> *** 3.80 ***<br/><br/>A buddy read with the most amazing KA addicts at BB&B's attic! </b><br/><br/>Another KA book, another hot couple, an alpha male with Neanderthal manner, a lost girl in a tough situation, and a struggle to find trust in humanity and each other... They are both damaged, craving what most take for granted, but seems forever out of reach for the two of them... Will Lady Luck look favorable upon them at least this one time? <br/><br/>Well, this is KA we are talking about and her books come with a Happily Ever A</span>
  <span id="freeText12314166507452318553" style="display:none"><b> *** 3.80 ***<br /><br />A buddy read with the most amazing KA addicts at BB&amp;B's attic! </b><br /><br />Another KA book, another hot couple, an alpha male with Neanderthal manner, a lost girl in a tough situation, and a struggle to find trust in humanity and each other... They are both damaged, craving what most take for granted, but seems forever out of reach for the two of them... Will Lady Luck look favorable upon them at least this one time? <br /><br />Well, this is KA we are talking about and her books come with a Happily Ever After guarantee!!! This is one of the reasons we keep coming back for more, because after she puts her characters through the wringer, gives them some tough trails and tribulations, gets them hurt, kidnapped and shot at, there better be some candy cane sweet ending for most, if not all good guys, or there will be only desolation and no insensitive to come back for more....<br /><br />As in the previous books in this particular series, it could have used some editing and been cut down by about 100 pages. But even with the extra, not needed in the least description of the hygiene routines of our heroes, KA did it again and I could not put the book down - I wanted to know what happens and in this specific book, WHAT THE HELLS IS IN THIS TAPE THAT DISTURBED THEM ALL SO MUCH??? Details, KA, inquiring minds need to know! <br /><br />This is a contemporary romance with crude language and if you have an issue with demeaning terms to women, this book is not for you. However, if you can get past the language of a felon who has just gotten out of prison, the romance is worth reading, and the two main characters have a ton of chemistry and sizzle!!! This is not for my feminist friends or sheltered young folks. For all the rest, who like their Romances on the cruder side of realistic, this is a fun read! <br /><br />I hope you all have cuddled up with a nice book for the weekend and may you all have a great reading experience! Happy reading, y'all!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12314166507452318553" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_639131198" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/639131198" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/639131198?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Kristen Ashley Fans, Romance</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17755575-wendy-sthoughts?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer639131198" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4580094608723569079"><b>5 Getting Your Dream Stars<br/>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free </i><br/>A few weeks ago I saw a promotion saying The Gamble was free. Well, that being a favorite in one of my favorite Kristen Ashely series…it started me on a path of re-reads of the entire series. The first three entries of the Colorado Mountain series were part of that Golden Year of Publishing for Ashley, 2011. It was during that time she put out twenty-one books…<br/><br/>Yup…Amazing… <br/><br/>Lady Luck has been a fan favorite forever…it has everything and more…And wh</b></span>
  <span id="freeText4580094608723569079" style="display:none"><b>5 Getting Your Dream Stars<br>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free </i><br>A few weeks ago I saw a promotion saying The Gamble was free. Well, that being a favorite in one of my favorite Kristen Ashely series…it started me on a path of re-reads of the entire series. The first three entries of the Colorado Mountain series were part of that Golden Year of Publishing for Ashley, 2011. It was during that time she put out twenty-one books…<br><br>Yup…Amazing… <br><br>Lady Luck has been a fan favorite forever…it has everything and more…And when I say that I am not kidding.<br><br>It has two main characters who have lived a tortured life, mirroring in many ways the same pain. It addresses racism, corruption, and inequities just to name a few. Those factors would normally be enough to give a story substance…but in Kristen Ashley’s hands, she took it to another level. From the opening scene she gave us these people where we were drawn in and could not look away.<br>There are numerous reviews which will give you everything you need and I encourage you to read them…I am not one to re-invent the wheel…<br><br>But I will share a couple of observations. </b> Ashley’s talent in building her stories is very sneaky… she leads you to believe things have reached where they need to be and then slams you into something else… and then takes that something else and ties it up with a whole other theory seamlessly. To be able to come up with all of the intricacies to do this is telling…<br><br>She also has this way of writing scenes of loving, fu@king and just plain touching that make you want…want it all for yourself…but also so happy for the characters.<br><br>Ty and Lexi are extremely special and in all the reading I have done…there are very few couples who caused as many heart-stopping moments… moments where you stare at the page and just have to breathe to take the beauty of it all in. Ashley does this repeatedly and it comes at times where you don’t expect it…and that is her gift.<br><br>Ashley is also the master of introducing characters; people who she wants you to be concerned about, to ponder and wonder what their deal is…so that when she writes the next tale you are all in. In re-reading Lady Luck, the introduction of Chace and Faye was so strong, the set up was priming us to run to the bookstore and stand in line for a year to get Breathe.<br><br>So to sum this up, Lady Luck is a book to not let go…to hold onto all of the beauty it displays…It is a book of hope, love and everything Ashley. <br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><b>
  <i> I went on a Kristen Ashley Binge in 2013. I recently re-read The Gamble and it put me in the mood to do all of the Colorado Mountain Series...one of my favorite of hers. Since I was very new to Goodreads, I never dreamt of reviewing. <br><br>When I finish, I will be reviewing this time. </i>
</b><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11227041.The_Gamble__Colorado_Mountain___1_" title="The Gamble (Colorado Mountain, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer5108351480487490557">Side note: I'm adding a star after having some very wise women point out that Ty had a broken past and a lot of the things he did came out of that. And in the end, he was totally in love with "Mama" and would give her the world. <br/><br/>I'm still pissed that vaccuuming was vagina work, though. <br/><br/><b>Color me unpopular</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495984330ra/22872605.gif' width='400' height='190' alt='feminist' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>This is a like / hate book for me.   <span id="freeText5108351480487490557" style="display:none">Side note: I'm adding a star after having some very wise women point out that Ty had a broken past and a lot of the things he did came out of that. And in the end, he was totally in love with "Mama" and would give her the world. <br><br>I'm still pissed that vaccuuming was vagina work, though. <br><br><b>Color me unpopular</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495984330ra/22872605.gif" width="400" height="190" alt="feminist" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This is a like / hate book for me. And I get that it's my sh!t here. But I'm totes willing to claim that it's my sh!t.<br><br><b>Read for URR New Years 2017 Challenge, Interracial romance category</b><br><br><b>Series:</b>Yep<br><br><b>Sexy times:</b> Sweet baby Jesus...it's a KA. So yea. There's lots of it and lots of magic penises and vaginas. <br><br><b>Plan on reading more by the author: </b>Despite this review, yes. Like meth, bitches. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444748459ra/16547349.gif" width="400" height="210" alt="addicted" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Synopsis:</b>Ty is wrongly convicted of a crime and Lexie is sent by some arsehole dude she is tied to due to her former lover's lifestyle, to pick said Ty up from prison when he is let out. She picks him up, he says two words, then he basically insinuates she is a ho. (Note to self: bitch, that was your first clue you weren't gonna be totally down with this book.) Anyhoo, she agrees to marry him and I don't think I'm giving anything away, but if you think I am, then stop reading this review, ok? <br><br>Stuff goes down and by stuff, I mean a lot of never ending drama. And we have super alpha Ty and super goof Lexie. <br><br><b>Heroine:</b> Lexie. On one hand, she's doing the best she can with the skills and tools she's got. She brings light and sunshine and that IS a very good thing. <br><br>On the other hand, you apparently can keep a good woman down. She seems unable to flex her very capable self against the norms of a society that keeps women in the kitchen and cleaning up after her man. And she goes into this most willingly and she teaches this to her children ensuring the life of the patriarchy. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460395660ra/18735287.gif" width="352" height="261" alt="offended" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Hero:</b> Yes, I get it, KA's heroes are anti-heroes. They are alpha. They are all "mine". They are cavemen. That's fine. But this one...well, he is more than that. He refers to women as "pussy", he kicks his woman out of the house for one perceived wrong, he refuses to do vagina work, and then he's this wonderful, caring, man. I'd probably kick him in the dinger first chance I got. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495984330ra/22872606.gif" width="400" height="208" alt="good day" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But I totally get that he was all in with Lexie and she was his. And he was hot as hell to boot.<br><br><b>Why it did or didn't work for me:</b> <br>I just cannot get past the woman's work / men's work message that pervades the book. Am I being OTT about it? Hell, I do not know. I just know that this rubbed me the wrong way. I'm not down with pussy referred to as a chain. And I am also not down with women in the kitchen. And only women in the kitchen. Especially when men are watching the game. Could we get any more broad strokes here? Please. <br><br>At the same time, the story is heartwarming and the connection between the H/h is fantastic...not toe curling fantastic, but still, it's something. This was a diverting read at best. Definitely not the best of the KAs. <br><br>Signed, <br><b>
  <i>Riding the meh train for this one</i>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer672561879" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6085130303139644661"><i>Originally posted on </i><a href='http://thebooknympho.com/2016/04/audio-review-lady-luck-by-kristen-ashley/' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Book Nympho</a><br/><br/>Lexie Berry is told by a low-life named Shift to pick up Ty Walker from a California prison. He will deliver the next set of instructions once she arrives. Yeah, there's a reason this guy's called Shift as Ty's next agenda item is a doozy.<br/><br/>I won't rehash what happens next (you should have the pleasure of discovering that yourself) or their histories but trust they both have interesting ones. While their first meeting was bizarre, it was also kismet. What comes </span>
  <span id="freeText6085130303139644661" style="display:none"><i>Originally posted on </i><a href="http://thebooknympho.com/2016/04/audio-review-lady-luck-by-kristen-ashley/" rel="nofollow noopener">The Book Nympho</a><br /><br />Lexie Berry is told by a low-life named Shift to pick up Ty Walker from a California prison. He will deliver the next set of instructions once she arrives. Yeah, there's a reason this guy's called Shift as Ty's next agenda item is a doozy.<br /><br />I won't rehash what happens next (you should have the pleasure of discovering that yourself) or their histories but trust they both have interesting ones. While their first meeting was bizarre, it was also kismet. What comes next is a funny, sometimes poignant and always interesting journey for the two of them. Both get something out of the deal they forge that will help them carve out a new path but they never counted on sticking or developing a romantic connection.<br /><br />It's hard not to like Lexie who is extremely loyal and despite all of the hard knocks she's received in life still maintains an infectious sense of optimism. Ty is more taciturn but even he can't help being positively affected by Lexie. The narrator does a very good job of distinguishing the new characters and I loved her depiction of Lexie.<br /><br />I really enjoyed this story, a lot. As with all the other books I've read in the series, it's highly addictive. Ashley just knows how to tell a story. My only criticism is with the descriptive language used by Ty for women. It was a huge turnoff...nothing romantic or seductive about it. Otherwise, this was a really fine story. 4.5 stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="6085130303139644661" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13179570519671793972">Spoilers ahead<br/>Reread again<br/>Still had my same issues from previously but I absolutely love this book and the mcs<br/><br/><br/>---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br/>Reread 13-11-19<br/>Gah I love this book so freaking much! This is one of a handful of books which always make me buy KA's books, the hope for another Ty and Lexie make it hard to give up on this author even with H's I absolutely hate like Keaton(y'all know I had to say it 😂)<br/><br/><br/>8-4-19<br/><br/>Reread # hmmmm I've stoppe</span>
  <span id="freeText13179570519671793972" style="display:none">Spoilers ahead<br />Reread again<br />Still had my same issues from previously but I absolutely love this book and the mcs<br /><br /><br />---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br />Reread 13-11-19<br />Gah I love this book so freaking much! This is one of a handful of books which always make me buy KA's books, the hope for another Ty and Lexie make it hard to give up on this author even with H's I absolutely hate like Keaton(y'all know I had to say it 😂)<br /><br /><br />8-4-19<br /><br />Reread # hmmmm I've stopped counting. Still love this one as in really love it! Still not a fan of Ty and him saying"pussy" in reference to women but this remains one of my top favorite books if not my #1 favorite.<br />----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br /><br />Reread 11-02-19-------After reading Free by KA, I had to reread this to remind myself why I even picked up a KA book in the first place. At the end of this,coming off the high that Ty and Lexie delivered I'm convinced that KA did not write Free..... Nuh uh the author who gave this to me would never deliver something like Free so it's evident that........the aliens did it.....I'm sticking to that! This as usual is allllllll the damn things. Absolutely still a favorite!<br /><br />***-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------***<br /><br />Lady luck has played with Lexie all her life,from a crap childhood ,to happiness with Ella, then taking a chance on Ella's son and him getting mixed up in bad shit that led to him being dead and her doing favors for a bad guy. One of those favors was picking up Ty Walker from prison. Ty proposes a fake marriage that he'll pay Lexie for so that he could pursue his vengeance. Lexie agrees and Mr and Mrs Walker head back to Carnal.<br /><br />I loved,loved,loved Lexie. I don't think I've ever read an h who took care of her man like Lexie did with Ty. With both their shitty childhood's she set out to create a home for him. Within days of her fake marriage it was clear she already had feelings for Ty. She was funny sweet loving but still managed to throw sass and have a backbone while being the wife of a seriously Alpha alpha male. When Ty screwed up huge and went to Lexie on that beach she proved her strength because she somehow resisted his apologies. I'd have caved at the first "mama" 😂<br /><br />Tyrell Walker had a shitty run of luck. He went from living the good life, getting pussy having money,good friends and a stable job to being locked away for a crime he didn't commit. All because some whacked police officers didn't like the black part of his makeup and needed a fall guy for their bad shit. He was understandably bitter and determined to get his vengeance. As much as I loved Ty and melted at every "Mama" throughout this book he said some seriously dumb shit sometimes. He messed up twice with Lexie by sprouting some bs thankfully after the dramatic reunion after their second blowup he learnt his lesson and only gave goodness to his wife. One of my major peeves with Ty though was his penchance for referring to women as pussy. It aggravated me to no end every time he did this but in the end the good that was Ty Walker far out weighed the bad that was his pussy preference.<br /><br />With bad guy cops floundering trying to cover up their bad guy duties and some bad ass good guys who had his back there was no end to the excitement in this one. <br /><br />While we are told Ty liked to get himself some and he took care of his women the only one we saw was bitch face Misty who Ty spent days(5 years previously) with and who should've been his alibi but bitch face Misty was working with the bad guys all so she could get Detective Chace Keaton.<br /><br />This is my favorite book in the series with one of my favorite epilogues of all time and also one of my favorite books of all time (pussy references non withstanding) It was emotional,sweet,funny and wonderfully written. I'm not sure why the phrase "mama" isn't used in more romance books because I melted every damn time I heard it but then again not every romance hero is Ty Walker so it's best to leave that endearment here. All in all this was as much a pleasure to reread now as it was on other occasions that I read it!<br /><br /><br /><br />“Down to my bones, mama, right back at you.” #swooooooooon!!!!!!!!<br /><br /><br /><br />*I've ever been hopeful that KA would deliver at least a novella with Sam Sterling. I've still got my fingers crossed that at some point that goodness will be delivered.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13179570519671793972" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer240824246" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5561787906859276137"><br/><b> Audiobook Review: 08/1/14</b><br/><br/>The audiobook is phenomenal! I didn't think I could love this story anymore than I already did, but Emma Taylor's fabulous narration took it to another level! She gets all of it! She gets the characters, she gets KA's writing, she knows how this book should be read! A highlight of the narration was for a character that I liked when I read the <i>Lady Luck</i> the first few times, but now I love him as much as any featured KA alpha hero. Angel Pena! For those of you who have re</span>
  <span id="freeText5561787906859276137" style="display:none"><br /><b> Audiobook Review: 08/1/14</b><br /><br />The audiobook is phenomenal! I didn't think I could love this story anymore than I already did, but Emma Taylor's fabulous narration took it to another level! She gets all of it! She gets the characters, she gets KA's writing, she knows how this book should be read! A highlight of the narration was for a character that I liked when I read the <i>Lady Luck</i> the first few times, but now I love him as much as any featured KA alpha hero. Angel Pena! For those of you who have read the book, you know who he is and what part he plays in the story. Emma Taylor made me fall in love with him. I understand him better than I ever did and never realized how funny he was, until I listened to her portray him with her voice. I don't mean that his voice is funny, but rather that the character KA created is hysterical, and I didn't really see that until I listened to the book. I could listen to his dialogue over and over. Emma Taylor gives him a brilliant, very authentic Mexican accent, and makes him witty, strong, charming, confident and unbelievably appealing! He is one hot cop and a hero in every respect! You can say what you like, but Kristen Ashley is her own brand and has created a genre of sorts and <i>Lady Luck</i> really showcases her talent. <br /><br />Anyhoo, if you get a chance, have a listen, your ears will thank you! <br /><br /><b>Original Review: 1/17/12</b><br /><b> 5 HUGE STARS!! </b> Intense, passionate, compelling and I LOVED IT!! <br /><br />From the first page to the last, it was outstanding. This book hit all the right buttons for me. Ty, WOW, he was a powerful, intriguing, yumtious character. Like the calm before the storm, I was never quite sure how he was going to react. Lexie was sassy, sexy, funny, and just delightful. She knows where she came from, where she’s been, and what she wants. She sees Ty’s power, good looks, but beneath all that, she sees a man that’s been wronged, and he needs someone he can trust. He is a pillar of strength, and she wants to be his pillar, the woman that he can lean on. Lexie and Ty were magic together, their personalities fed off each other and it was a beautiful to read. <br /><br />In the other books in the series, Tate and Max hammered and yammered during sex, and quite effectively I might add. Ty didn’t have to say anything, he let his eyes, fingers and tongue speak for him, and then pounded his way home! SWEET JESUS, by the time he was done with his sexual conquest, I WAS TWITCHING!! I twitched a lot; because the man was insatiable…he had quite…ahem…the appetite! <br /><br />What made this read so special was going home to Carnal and the people we love! Tate was there in all his glory and played a huge part in the plot. Ty and Tate…awesomeness to the max, oh yeah and Max made a brief appearance too! Start to finish, I was captivated, and had a hard time putting my Kindle down.<br /> <br />Kristen Ashley does real so well that at times I felt as if I was hurled into the story, and was lurking in the background as it played out. Two scenes in particular, just tugged at my heart, nearly ripped it out of my chest. The first was when Ty came to the salon… he was breathtaking, Lexie was breathtaking, THEY were breathtaking…WOW!! The other one was when two amazing men stood atop a Colorado mountain and expressed what their friendship meant to each other…VERY POTENT! When you read it, you will understand.<br /><br />The epilogue, I don’t even want to go there, satisfying is an understatement, Ty and Lexie were so deserving of it and it had me grinning like a Cheshire cat. Kristen Ashley knows what her readers want and she delivers it in a big way. Chace is up next and I’m already yearning for him, just like Faye!<br /><br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13734703816731206255">It's Friday and that means......another KA book with my girls at <a>Buddies Books & Baubles</a>. <br/><br/><b>4.5 Your Nightmare was My Dream Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Me the very beginning of this book</b><br/><br/><i>Um…our hero Ty has no clue how to use a verb or a noun. He grunts and barely puts two syllables together. How am I supposed to read a book with him in it.</i><br/><br/><b>Just a little while later….</b><br/><br/><i>Oh look he knows more than two words and I thought that would be better but OMG it is worse. He pretty much refers to stuff in terms of pussy and dick and I’m</i></span>
  <span id="freeText13734703816731206255" style="display:none">It's Friday and that means......another KA book with my girls at <a>Buddies Books &amp; Baubles</a>. <br /><br /><b>4.5 Your Nightmare was My Dream Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Me the very beginning of this book</b><br /><br /><i>Um…our hero Ty has no clue how to use a verb or a noun. He grunts and barely puts two syllables together. How am I supposed to read a book with him in it.</i><br /><br /><b>Just a little while later….</b><br /><br /><i>Oh look he knows more than two words and I thought that would be better but OMG it is worse. He pretty much refers to stuff in terms of pussy and dick and I’m growing concerned that I am not going to like Ty if this keeps up.</i><br /><br /><b>But then a smidgen later…</b><br /><br />Ty becomes interesting and the plot of the story heats up. See Alexa Berry was roped into picking him up from jail but she didn’t know the rest of what was promised to Ty Walker….and it is going to be a big surprise.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Alexa Anne Berry. Dallas resident. Buyer at Lowenstein’s department store. I need everything you can get on her.” <br />“Walker, I’m a bounty hunter, not a PI,” Jackson reminded him.<br /> “You got resources. You got connections. I’m askin’ you to use them.” <br />Pause then, “Who is this woman?”<br /> “I’m marryin’ her tomorrow.</i>
</blockquote><br />Well tickle me pink and call me a peony I know right at this moment in the story I’m going to love it. Instant marriage of convenience to something more is one of my favorite tropes when done right.<br /><br />Don’t worry Ty gets a vocabulary and while I think he is the most crass of all the KA alphas to date he has moments of utter tenderness too. It became clear after he learned who Alexa’s last and only boyfriend ended up dead and the life he led while alive that Ty was a diamond in the rough.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“So, you know when the limit’s up on love?” he asked, and I felt my chest depress as the profound weight of his question hit me. <br />“No,” I whispered. <br />“Right. No. No one does. Not you. Not me. No one. You loved him, you believed in him. Far’s you were concerned, he didn’t take those hits, the day after, he coulda got his head outta his ass and done right by you. You held onto that belief. Nothin’ wrong with that except the fact that he never manned up, and that’s on him not on you.”</i>
</blockquote><br />So yay we get a dirty talking hero and one of my favorite heroines because she doesn’t spend much time pitying anything in her life and for the most part she is bubbly in full of happiness and sunshine….I totally understand that girl. Beside that Lexie is a little bit goofy and I totally get that. I loved her outgoing, sassy talking, don’t take crap from no one attitude and how she lives her life large. <br /><br />I loved their love story but I also enjoyed the side story of Ty finding out a way to get justice for the five years he spent in prison for a crime he didn’t commit and coming to terms with what it means to live free and how to let some stuff from his past go. He wasn’t always good at it and he totally screwed up a few times but overall Ty might be my new favorite alpha….well at least in the Colorado Mountain series that it.<br /></span>

A very pleased pleasure sigh!</b><br/><br/>I just finished this as an 22 hrs audiobook and it was a GREAT one.   <span id="freeText838644900652467090" style="display:none"><i>Written October 31, 2014</i><br><br><b>4 1/2 Stars - Just as good as expected. A very pleased pleasure sigh!</b><br><br>I just finished this as an 22 hrs audiobook and it was a GREAT one. He was wrongly imprisoned and she is tricked by a former (dead) boyfriend's fake (sh@t) friend that she just have to take her car and drive this stately, big, beautiful black man where he wants to go. And Ty he feels something odd and new stabbing in the heart region each time this laughing kind woman <u>shares</u> with him.<br><br><br>***********************************************************<br><br><b>...I almost forgot the side-plot:</b><br>The suspense story here, the topic besides the romance, was of course to establish some justice, vengeance and repayment, about of the criminal act, and more nasty events, Ty innocently was accused was locked up in prison for in full five years. ~ It was very clever, with slick villains and also slightly complicated. In the end very dramatic and exciting thrillig.<br><br>***********************************************************<br><br><b>This was a grand love-story about sharing, trust and to give</b>. Give more than you get and try to keep the good things you get in life. <br><blockquote>“What you need to give me is to know it is not about you, it’s about me, you gotta suck it up and stand by me, you gotta know, in the end, I’ll work my ass off to make it all worth it to you and you gotta always remember I love you and I have never, not once, said those words to any breathing soul so you also gotta know what that means.” </blockquote><br><i>Lady Luck</i> as an audiobook was so very beautiful and charming sweet to listening to. As always, a lot of dialogue and also very funny banters. A healthy dose of cave man's statements from Ty and that sexy gruff groan that only real alpha male gets up. ~ Of course was it hot in the bedroom when this amazing man took care of his woman. Oh yeah, really steaming hot.<br><br>These MC's, Ty and Lexie, are characters to instantly start to love and feel for. Ordinary people in an ordinary (I assume) small Colorado town. Ordinary people who just wants to make a good life for themself and their loved ones. <br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Couple%20in%20love/d9094919-e188-4e65-8f47-aca3f0fa25b6_zpseaf3faf9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414778206i/11691526.jpg" alt=" photo d9094919-e188-4e65-8f47-aca3f0fa25b6_zpseaf3faf9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>‘…It was an arms crushing me to his body, heads slanting, mouths opened, tongues invading, toes curling, knees weakening, bones dissolving, deep, wet, hungry, carnal kiss. It seemed to last forever but that forever was not near long enough.’</blockquote><br>**********************************************************<br><br><b>A lovely, romantic, hugely long book as warmed my heart</b> and made me want to read, or listening to, a lot more of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> fantastic romances. Books dealing with these adult (their 30 years party are passed a few years ago), simple but yet unique, so damn brave, loving, wonderful men and women. People I would love to spend time with, have as my family etc.<br><br>...I need much more about all these Colorado mountain chicks and their adorable alpha males. <br><br><b>I LIKE - enjoyed, giggled and loved it for 22 hours</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="838644900652467090" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('KkuHGpLMlBXN5VzC4mJeLGEsQn3rJs95HUq1/A3gwMv24OqAUWAEO+zOf/k03o5Hl/Vq++VytmfcbOFpmJS10g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('dWHnlyEIxqFPGgZKAdfkrzBPwSie3bkIDxEQbH5f5JqpyooN4qRWj24xJXHXazTExpbprpCJwBbON0T56yuRgw==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer7006416165557980185">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br/><br/>Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends a</span>
  <span id="freeText7006416165557980185" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/18115826-lady-luck">Quotes from Lady Luck</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;&lt;…&gt;When I was done speaking I felt his body had gone still again, stone still. <br />And silent. <br />Then he asked quietly, "Nightmare?" <br />"Nightmare," I replied firmly. <br />Ty didn't move. <br />By a miracle, I held it together. <br />Then he moved but it was to rest his chin on my shoulder and I closed my eyes because I needed him to go, go, go so I could fall apart again on my own. <br />Then he said, "Your nightmare, mama, was my dream." <br />My heart clenched. <br />He kept going. "Never had a home until you gave me one." <br />My breath started sticking. <br />"Never had anyone give to me the way you gave to me." <br />My breath stopped sticking and clogged. <br />"Never thought of findin' a woman who I wanted to have my baby." <br />Oh God. <br />"Never had light in my life, never, not once, I lived wild but I didn't burn bright until you shined your light on me." <br />Oh God. <br />"Whacked, fuckin' insane, but, at night, you curled in front of me, didn't mind I did that time that wasn't mine 'cause it meant I walked out to you." <br />He had to stop. He had to. <br />He didn't. <br />"Your nightmare," he whispered, turned his head and against my neck he finished, "my dream."&lt;…&gt;&rdquo;</span>

When I do, shoot me with it.”<br />“What?” she whispered.<br />“I’m facin’ another hour and a half of your music. I’d rather be dead.”<br />Silence then, “Shut up.&rdquo;</span>
